	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/SecureMailer.class.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/SecureMailer.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/SecureMailer.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/SecureMailer.class.php') != '7a8f60b68d9573f6935e9996c1363a413b44ad40') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/SecureMailer.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/SecureMailer.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/SecureMailer.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/SecureMailer.class.php') !== '7a8f60b68d9573f6935e9996c1363a413b44ad40') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/SecureMailer.class.php') !== '3f27a5f75ef50226f9f97683bea1660422557a45') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/SecureMailer.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/SecureMailer.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/SecureMailer.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/SecureMailer.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/SecureMailer.class.php') !== '7a8f60b68d9573f6935e9996c1363a413b44ad40') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/SecureMailer.class.php');

if (!is_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') != '4afb600eb0c2b6a1b0cc04e769f31708bc73009e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') !== '4afb600eb0c2b6a1b0cc04e769f31708bc73009e') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') !== 'bef1fe212f0e9c3aef10a24a1c6a65f55b749bd6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') !== '4afb600eb0c2b6a1b0cc04e769f31708bc73009e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') != '73eaf2fcf2b50299b6446f9dbb9a825e19d02446') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '73eaf2fcf2b50299b6446f9dbb9a825e19d02446') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '1a409eebb99dfd49ede9f2d27e2057bce8a28be9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '73eaf2fcf2b50299b6446f9dbb9a825e19d02446') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') != 'ca198a1ff2708e45b7b022e4d2b80154a1959b5a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== 'ca198a1ff2708e45b7b022e4d2b80154a1959b5a') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== 'ca198a1ff2708e45b7b022e4d2b80154a1959b5a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') != '1c0e733093946d303d4731b4c9fa23f503864d1a') {

	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {

	}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '1c0e733093946d303d4731b4c9fa23f503864d1a') {

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/xml_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php') !== '0e3e499eb50499dbd2ce8b9c20763153dbfcceeb') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php') !== '033745cd36224b0f841af3ed4109f8847468d7c6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/xml_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/xml_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/xml_utils.inc.php') !== '0e3e499eb50499dbd2ce8b9c20763153dbfcceeb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/xml_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}
